Would be cool if one day Dhar Maan released a video where the ending is just sad. There is no happy ending, but sometimes that just happens, and that is okay. It would have to be done right, but it would be nice to have a message on this channel that bad things just happen sometimes, it's okay to cry about it and it is okay to feel sad.  Life is always about the ups and downs, these videos always seem to end on the up's. But in some situations there is no high point to leave on, for example. Sometimes you say goodbye to a friend, it sucks and it is sad, sometimes there is nothing you can do about it. It can be shown that bad things like this happen, and sometimes all you can do after is grieve. I feel like a nice story about the growth of a friendship from beginning to end would bw nice, then to see the goodbye happen, and maybe they never see each other again. We watch the two begin a new stage in their lives apart from each other, and that is okay. They both struggle, and miss each other. But eventually they move on to make new friends while creating a new life. This could show people it is okay to just be sad sometimes, but learn to not let it consume your whole life, and be able to keep moving forward.
